     <section class="content-section" id="more">
      <div class="row">
       <div class="col-xs-6">
        <h2>
         Details
        </h2>
        <div class="content-block lg toggle">
         <div class="description toggle-content">
          <p class="description-item-number">
           ITEM#: 429710
          </p>
          <br/>
          <b>
           Product Features
          </b>
          <ul>
           <li>
            Try wrapping your head around this challenging traditional lotus puzzle from Cambodia
           </li>
           <li>
            Puzzle is designed to stretch your mental abilities to the limit
           </li>
           <li>
            Produced by the artisans of Rehab Craft Cambodia, these puzzles were created by people learning to overcome their disabilities and those coping with landmine accidents and the tragedy that accompanies it
           </li>
           <li>
            Handcarved from Sralan and Lagerstroemia wood
           </li>
           <li>
            Lotus shape
           </li>
           <li>
            Traditional etched designs
           </li>
           <li>
            Composite of varying textures and colors of wood
           </li>
           <li>
            Measures 3.25 inches high x 2.25 inches diameter
           </li>
           <li>
            Made in Cambodia
           </li>
          </ul>
          <b>
           Story Behind the Art
          </b>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          This wonderful product is created on Phnom Penh Cambodia. It currently  employees Cambodian landmine survivors as well and people with disabilities, there is a total of 50 artisans that work with us on this project. Vocational training is provided to potential producer staff. Those who reach the required standard are offered permanent employment through handicraft products and Cambodian hand?woven silk. This is for landmine survivors and other people with physical disabilities.  The program includes a credit scheme supporting sustainable self-employment for Cambodians with disabilities. This program aims to provide practical assistance to self-employed Cambodian craftspeople, through a revolving fund that supports its own expansion through sale
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a _blank="" href="http://www.overstock.com/cgi-bin/d2.cgi?SEC_IID=12756&amp;PAGE=STATICPAGE&amp;PAGE_ID=2432" target="">
           <span class="links">
            What is Worldstock?
           </span>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <i>
           The handcrafted touch of artisan skill creates variations in color, size and design. If buying two of the same item, slight differences should be expected. Note: Color discrepancies may occur between this product and your computer screen.
          </i>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <i>
           Imported
          </i>
          <br/>
          <br/>

          </b>

          <header>
           Different quality between items
          </header>
          <div class="bd">
           <div class="ratings">
            <span class="stars" data-rating="3">
             <i class="os-icon os-icon-star-two star-1">
             </i>
             <i class="os-icon os-icon-star-two star-2">
             </i>
             <i class="os-icon os-icon-star-two star-3">
             </i>
             <i class="os-icon os-icon-star-two star-4">
             </i>
             <i class="os-icon os-icon-star-two star-5">
             </i>
            </span>
           </div>
           <p>
            I bought two of these as christmas gifts and of course played with each before giving them away. The quality between the two was vastly different. the one was beautiful and all the pieces fit perfectly, but the other was very loose (the pieces almost just fell apart when you were trying to take it apart or put it back together).  The one that was good quality was a beautiful piece to have out, but the one with very loose pieces just looked funny sitting out on a table as it looked like it would fall apart if someone touched it. I ended up gifting the good quality one and kept the worse one for myself as i wouldnt have given it as a gift and am too lazy to return it.
           </p>

     <section class="content-section" id="shipping">
      <div class="row">
       <div class="col-xs-12">
        <h2>
         Shipping &amp; Returns
        </h2>
        <div class="content-block toggle">
         <div class="shipping-returns toggle-content">
          <h5>
           Shipping:
          </h5>
          <p>
           Usually leaves our warehouse in 1-2 business days. *
          </p>
          <img alt="ApoFpo able" border="0" src="http://ak1.ostkcdn.com/img/mxc/apo_fpo_logo.gif"/>
          <h5>
           Standard Return Policy:
          </h5>
          <p>
           Items must be returned in new or unused condition and contain all original materials included with the shipment.
           <a class="more cboxElement" data-cbox-height="500" data-cbox-iframe="true" data-cbox-width="980" data-omni-name="Shipping &amp; Returns" data-omni-on="click" data-omni-val="PRODPG:MoreDetails" data-omni-var="eVar4" href="https://help.overstock.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/1">
            More
    Details
           </a>
          </p>
          <!-- Adding Final Sale text, remove on March 3, 2012 -->
          <p>
           FINAL SALE EXCLUSION: Items marked as FINAL SALE are not
    returnable unless the problem you experience is the result of our error.
          </p>
          <h5>
           Shipping Information:
          </h5>
          <p>
           Our standard shipping method is ground shipping. We also offer expedited shipping for most items. Your final
						shipping cost and estimated delivery timeframe will be available at checkout.
           <br/>
           <a class="more cboxElement" data-cbox-height="500" data-cbox-iframe="true" data-cbox-width="980" data-omni-name="Shipping &amp; Returns" data-omni-on="click" data-omni-val="PRODPG:StandardShippingDetails" data-omni-var="eVar4" href="https://help.overstock.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/7">
            Standard shipping details
           </a>
           <br/>
           <a class="more cboxElement" data-cbox-height="500" data-cbox-iframe="true" data-cbox-width="980" data-omni-name="Shipping &amp; Returns" data-omni-on="click" data-omni-val="PRODPG:ExpeditedShipping" data-omni-var="eVar4" href="https://help.overstock.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/727">
            Expedited shipping details
           </a>
          </p>
          <!-- PP_01_SHIP_EXP -->
          <!--&lt;h5&gt;Expedited Shipping: &lt;/h5&gt;
					&lt;p&gt;We offer Next Day, 2 Day, and 3 Day shipping for most items. Expedited shipping is not available for items being shipped to PO Boxes or APO/FPO destinations. For more information on this please view our Expedited Shipping page.
					&lt;br&gt;&lt;a class="more" href="javascript:void window.open('https://help.overstock.com/app/answers/detail/a_id/727', 'Policy', 'width=1024,height=768,resizable=yes,menubar=yes,location=no,status=no,scrollbars=yes');"&gt;More details&lt;/a&gt;
					&lt;/p&gt;-->
          <p class="terms">
           * For your protection, all orders are screened for security purposes. If your order is selected for review, our Loss Prevention Team may contact you by phone or email. There may be a two business day delay to process your order.
          </p>
          <p class="terms">
           ** Most Oversize orders are delivered within 1-4 weeks. Some orders may take 6 weeks to be
					delivered.
          </p>

jQuery(document).ready(function() {
    var $promoBanner = jQuery('.grid-container-promo .banner'),
        $cambarPrompt = jQuery('.cambar-active-prompt'),
        $promoCID = "140483",
        camUrl = 'https://api.overstock.com/cambar/' + $promoCID;

    if ($promoCID) {

        var ajaxComplete = function(data) {
            var camCluboCheck = -1,
                $isProductPage = jQuery('#product-page');

            if (typeof data == 'string') {
                data = $.parseJSON(data);
            }
            if (data.camBar) {
                camCluboCheck = data.camBar.indexOf('Club O');
                $promoBanner.show();
                if (data.camExcludeValues) {
                    data.camExcludeValues = data.camExcludeValues.replace('Extra 5% Off', 'Doorbusters');
                }
                var camExclude = '';
                if (data.camSavings) {camExclude += data.camSavings + ' '}
                if (data.camCheckout) {camExclude += data.camCheckout + ' '}
                if (data.camExcludeMessage) {camExclude += data.camExcludeMessage + ' '}
                if (data.camExcludeValues) {camExclude += data.camExcludeValues + ' '}
                if (data.camStackable) {camExclude += data.camStackable}

                var camMessage = '',
                    pageCIDUrl = '';

                if (data.camCustomer) {camMessage += data.camCustomer + ' '}
                if (data.camBar) {camMessage += data.camBar + ' '}
                if (camMessage) {
                    $promoBanner.find('.heading-text').text(camMessage);
                    $cambarPrompt.find('.cambar-active-message').text(camMessage);
                    
                    // SITE_01_CAMBAR_VAR 
                    pageCIDUrl = document.URL;
                    pageCIDUrl = pageCIDUrl.toLowerCase();


                    if (pageCIDUrl.indexOf("?cid=") != -1 || pageCIDUrl.indexOf("&amp;cid=") != -1) {
                           $cambarPrompt.show();
                        setTimeout(function(){
                           $cambarPrompt.hide();
                        },3000)
                    }
                    
 

                }
                if (camExclude) {
                    camExclude += '&lt;i class="os-icon-x-long os-icon"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;'
                    $promoBanner.find('.disclaimer').html(camExclude);
                }

                if (typeof responsivePage != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; camMessage) {
                    var newMSSCambar = '&lt;div class="mss-cambar-area"&gt;' + '&lt;div class="heading-text"&gt;' + camMessage + '&lt;/div&gt;' + '&lt;div class="disclaimer"&gt;' + camExclude + '&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
                    jQuery('#newo-hd').append(newMSSCambar);

                    jQuery('.mss-cambar-area .heading-text').on('click', function() {
                        jQuery('.mss-cambar-area .disclaimer').slideToggle();
                    });
                }

            }
            if (camCluboCheck &gt; -1 &amp;&amp; $isProductPage) {
                var cluboCouponPrct = data.camBar.split('%')[0] + '%';
                jQuery('#cluboCoups').addClass('clubo-show');
                jQuery('.pp-clubo-coup-pcnt').text(cluboCouponPrct);
                jQuery('#cluboDflt').addClass('clubo-hide');
            }

        };
        jQuery.support.cors = true;

        jQuery.ajax({
            url: camUrl,
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function(data) {
                ajaxComplete(data);
            }
        });
    }
});

os.checkPromoBar = function() {
	
	var $hdHeader = jQuery('#newo-hd.hd-ss-b'),
		$hdPromoContainer = $hdHeader.find('.grid-container-promo'),
		$hdPromo = $hdHeader.find('.hd-shippingbanner a'),
		$hdBanner = $hdHeader.find('.banner'),
		$hdDisclaimer = $hdHeader.find('.disclaimer')

	return {
		init: function() {
            var _this = this;
			var checkPromoBar = _.debounce(_this.calcPromoBar, 300);
						
			if($hdBanner.length){
				jQuery(window).resize(checkPromoBar);
				$hdBanner.on('click.showdisclaimer',function(){
					$hdPromoContainer.addClass('promoCollapse');
					$hdHeader.on('mouseleave',function(){
						_this.calcPromoBar();
						$hdHeader.unbind('mouseleave');
					});
				})
				$hdDisclaimer.on('click.closebtn','i', function(e){
					e.stopPropagation();
					$hdPromoContainer.removeClass('promoCollapse');
				})
				_this.calcPromoBar();
			}
		},
		calcPromoBar: function(){
				$hdPromoContainer.removeClass('promoCollapse');
			if ($hdPromo.outerHeight() &gt; $hdPromoContainer.outerHeight()){
				$hdPromoContainer.addClass('promoCollapse');
			}else{
				$hdPromoContainer.removeClass('promoCollapse');	
			}
		}
	}
};

var runThis = new os.checkPromoBar();
runThis.init();

jQuery('#mini-cart').on('click.trackCheckout', 'a.btn-checkout-img', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    
    var gaChkoutLink = jQuery(this).attr('href');

    if (ga &amp;&amp; ga.trackingManager &amp;&amp; ga.trackingManager.getTrackingSessions) {
    
        var gaChkout = ga.trackingManager.getTrackingSessions(),
            gaObj = {};

        gaObj['sessions'] = gaChkout;
        gaObj['name'] = 'CHECKOUT_NOW';
        gaObj['option'] = (gaChkoutLink.indexOf("CHNOW") &gt; -1) ? 'HEADER' : 'MINI_CART';

        jQuery.ajax({
            url: '//www.overstock.com/api2/tracking/events/carts/checkouts',
            data: JSON.stringify(gaObj),
            type: 'PUT',
            contentType: 'application/json'
        });

    }

    window.location = gaChkoutLink;

});

   <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function() {

// Sign in Prompt
// SITE_01_PROMPT_JS
// Use this function to display a container similar to a tooltip but will only show once.

os.ItemContainerPrompt = function() {


    var settings = {
        startDelayTime: 3000,
        endDelayTime: 7000,
        itemContainer: '#user-signin-prompt',
        itemClose: '.close-x',
        itemException: '#user-account',
        itemID: "UserSignIn"

    };
	var autoCloseTimer;

    return {
        init: function(set) {
        	var _this = this;
        	
        	jQuery.extend(settings,set);

            settings.itemContainer = jQuery(settings.itemContainer);
            settings.itemClose = settings.itemContainer.find(settings.itemClose);
            settings.itemException = jQuery(settings.itemException);
            settings.itemID = 'sto' + settings.itemID;

			_this.checkInstance();

        },
        checkInstance: function(){
        	var _this = this;
			if (!localStorage[settings.itemID]){
				_this.openItemPrompt();
			
				settings.itemContainer.on('mouseenter',function(){
					_this.endTimer();
				});
				settings.itemContainer.on('mouseleave',function(){
					_this.startTimer();
				});
				settings.itemClose.on('click',function(){
					_this.closeItemPrompt();
				});
				settings.itemException.on('mouseover',function(){
					_this.closeItemPrompt();
				});	
			}
        },        
        openItemPrompt: function() {
        	var _this = this;
        	        	
			var startDelay = setTimeout(function(){
				settings.itemContainer.fadeIn('slow');			
				_this.startTimer();
			},settings.startDelayTime);
        },
        closeItemPrompt: function(action) {
        	var _this = this;
        	
			_this.endTimer();
			if (action === 'fade'){
				settings.itemContainer.fadeOut('slow');
			}else{
				settings.itemContainer.hide();
			}
			if (os.isLocalStorageEnabled()) {
			    localStorage.setItem(settings.itemID, true);
			}
        },
        startTimer: function(){
        	var _this = this;
        	
    		autoCloseTimer = setTimeout(function(){
				_this.closeItemPrompt('fade');
			},settings.endDelayTime);
        },
        endTimer: function() {
			clearTimeout(autoCloseTimer);
        }
    };
};
if (!IsLogged &amp;&amp; !localStorage.stoUserSignIn){
	var signInPrompt = new os.ItemContainerPrompt;
	signInPrompt.init();
};
   </script>

   <!-- Omail Subscribe -->
   <script>
    function submitOmail(init, isValidEmailAddress, GetURLParameter, blurAndFocus, getGroupId, submitLogic){
    this.init = function( config ){
        this.formID = config.formID;
        this.emailInput = config.emailInput;
        this.egID = config.egID;
        this.submitButton = config.submitButton;
        this.confirmInput = config.confirmInput;
        this.isDual = config.isDual;
        this.actionUrl = config.actionUrl;
        this.errorMsg = config.errorMsg;
        this.confirm = config.confirm;
        this.submitLogic();
    };

    this.isValidEmailAddress = function( emailAddress ) {
        var pattern = new RegExp(/^((([a-z]|\d|[!#\$%&amp;'\*\+\-\/=\?\^_`{\|}~]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])+(\.([a-z]|\d|[!#\$%&amp;'\*\+\-\/=\?\^_`{\|}~]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])+)*)|((\x22)((((\x20|\x09)*(\x0d\x0a))?(\x20|\x09)+)?(([\x01-\x08\x0b\x0c\x0e-\x1f\x7f]|\x21|[\x23-\x5b]|[\x5d-\x7e]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(\\([\x01-\x09\x0b\x0c\x0d-\x7f]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF]))))*(((\x20|\x09)*(\x0d\x0a))?(\x20|\x09)+)?(\x22)))@((([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])([a-z]|\d|-|\.|_|~|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])*([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])))\.)+(([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])([a-z]|\d|-|\.|_|~|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])*([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])))\.?$/i);
        return pattern.test(emailAddress);
    };

    this.GetURLParameter = function( sParam ){
        var sPageURL = window.location.search.substring(1);
        var sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&amp;');
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; sURLVariables.length; i++) 
        {
            var sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');
            if (sParameterName[0] == sParam) 
            {
                return sParameterName[1];
            }
        }
    };

    this.blurAndFocus = function(){
        var self = this;

        self.emailInput.on('focus', function(){
            if ( self.emailInput.val().toLowerCase() == 'enter email address' ){
                self.emailInput.val('');
            }
        });


        self.emailInput.on('blur', function(){
            if ( self.emailInput.val() === '' ){
                self.emailInput.val('Enter Email Address');
            }
        });

        if ( self.isDual === true ){
            self.confirmInput.on('focus', function(){
                if ( self.confirmInput.val() == 'Confirm Email Address'){
                    self.confirmInput.val('');
                }
            });              


            self.confirmInput.on('blur', function(){
                if ( self.confirmInput.val() === '' ){
                    self.confirmInput.val('Confirm Email Address');
                }
            });
        }
    };

    this.getGroupId = function(){
        var self = this;
        var omailURL = document.URL;
        //check for omail keyword in URL, this will be there when omail is searched for on overstock
        if ( typeof self.GetURLParameter('keywords') != 'undefined' ){
            var URLkeywords = self.GetURLParameter('keywords').toLowerCase();
            if ( URLkeywords.indexOf('omail') &gt; -1 ){
                self.egID.val('2364');
            }
        }

        // check if on communications preference page of my account
        if ( jQuery('#myAcct_alpha_com').hasClass('selected') ){
            self.egID.val('2374');
        }

        // check if user is on account setting page of my account
        if ( jQuery('#myAcct_alpha_acc').hasClass('selected') ){
            self.egID.val('1651');
        }

        //check referrer to see if user came from google
        if ( document.referrer.indexOf('http://www.google.com') &gt; -1 ){
            self.egID.val('2365');
        }


        //if group ID (egID) is in the URL 
        if ( omailURL.indexOf('egID') &gt; -1 ){
            var omailID = self.GetURLParameter('egID');
            self.egID.val(omailID);
        }

        //if s.egID exists
        if ( typeof s.egID != 'undefined' ){
            self.egID.val(s.egID);
        }
    };

    this.submitLogic = function(){
        var self = this;

        self.getGroupId();
        self.blurAndFocus();

        var theyMatch = 'go';

        jQuery(self.emailInput).keydown(function(event){    
            if(event.keyCode==13){
                jQuery(self.submitButton).trigger('click');
            }
        });
        
        jQuery(self.formID).submit(function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
        });

        jQuery( self.submitButton ).click(function( e ){
            e.preventDefault();
            if ( self.isDual === true ){
                // check to see if emails match
                var val1 = self.emailInput.val().toLowerCase();
                var val2 = self.confirmInput.val().toLowerCase();
                if ( val1 != val2 ){
                    if ( !jQuery('#matchErr').is(':visible') ){
                        var matchErr = '&lt;p id="matchErr" style="' + self.errorMsg + '"&gt;&lt;/p&gt;';
                        self.formID.before(matchErr);
                        jQuery('#matchErr').text('Emails Must Match');
                        jQuery.colorbox.resize();
                        theyMatch = 'stop';
                        if ( document.URL.indexOf('/coupons') &gt; -1 ){
                            jQuery(self.formID).prev('#matchErr').css('marginTop','-40px');
                        }
                        setTimeout(function(){
                            jQuery('#matchErr').remove();
                            jQuery.colorbox.resize();
                        }, 5000);

                    }
                } else{
                    jQuery('#matchErr').remove();
                    jQuery.colorbox.resize();
                    theyMatch = 'go';
                }
            }
            //if the email is good remove the error
            function addEmailError(){
                var emailErr = '&lt;p id="emailErr" style="' + self.errorMsg + '"&gt;&lt;/p&gt;';
                self.formID.before(emailErr);
                jQuery(self.formID).prev('#emailErr').text('Please Enter a Valid Email');
                jQuery.colorbox.resize();
                setTimeout(function(){
                    jQuery(self.formID).prev('#emailErr').remove();
                    jQuery.colorbox.resize();
                }, 5000);
            }

            if ( self.isValidEmailAddress( self.emailInput.val() ) ){
                jQuery('#emailErr').remove();
            } else{
                if ( !jQuery(self.formID).prev('#emailErr').is(':visible') ){
                    addEmailError();
                }
            }
            //if the email is good and they match then it's a go
            if ( self.isValidEmailAddress( self.emailInput.val() ) &amp;&amp; theyMatch == 'go'){
                jQuery.ajax({
                    url: self.actionUrl,
                    type: 'post',
                    data: self.formID.serialize(),
                    success: function( data ){
                        os.omailData = data;
                        if( data.success === false &amp;&amp; data.errorMessage != 'EMAIL_ALREADY_SUBSCRIBED' ){
                            if( data.errorMessage == 'INVALID_EMAIL' ){
                                addEmailError();
                            }
                            if ( data.errorMessage == 'OTHER_ERROR' ){
                                addEmailError();
                                jQuery('#emailErr').text('Oops, something went wrong');
                                jQuery.colorbox.resize();
                            }
                        } else{
                            // Track successful Omail
                            if(data.success === true){
                                var s = s || s_gi('overstock.com');
                                var sVars = {};
                                sVars.linkTrackVars = 'events';
                                sVars.linkTrackEvents = 'event14';
                                sVars.events = 'event14';
                                s.tl(this, 'o', 'Omail Signup Lightbox', sVars);                
                            }
                            if ( typeof self.confirm != 'function'){
                                jQuery.colorbox({
                                    href: "//www.overstock.com/80806/spage.html",
                                    width:420,
                                    scrolling: false,
                                    onComplete: function(){
                                        //clear email out
                                        self.emailInput.val('Enter Email Address');

                                        if ( data.errorMessage == 'EMAIL_ALREADY_SUBSCRIBED' ){
                                            jQuery('p.omailText').text('Looks like you\'re already signed up to receive some amazing deals!');
                                        }
                                        jQuery.colorbox.resize();
                                        jQuery('.omailContinue').click(function( e ){
                                            e.preventDefault();
                                            jQuery.colorbox.close();
                                        });
                                    }
                                });
                            } else{
                                self.confirm();
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            } 
        });

    };

}
   </script>

// Use this function to display either a colorbox or a new window with compare pricing information (compare/was/msrp)
os.ComparePricingColorbox = function() {

	var settings = {
		compareSugExact: {//At other retailer
			title: "What is \"At other retailer\"?",

			href: "http://www.overstock.com/compare-at"
		},

			title: "What is \"WAS\"?",
			href: "http://www.overstock.com/80046/static.html"
		},

			title: "What is \"MSRP\"?",
			href: "http://www.overstock.com/80047/static.html"

		}

				href: href,
				title: title,
				scrolling: true,

		},
		showNewWindow: function(href, title, thisEl){
			var windowName = 'PriceWindow',

			newWindowH = 400,
			newWindowL = (window.outerWidth-newWindowW) / 2,
			newWindowT = (window.outerHeight-newWindowH) / 2;

			window.open(href,windowName,'scrollbars=1,toolbar=1,location=1,statusbar=1,menubar=1,resizable=1,width='+newWindowW+',height='+newWindowH+',left='+newWindowL+',top='+newWindowT);
		}
	};
};

   <script>
    jQuery(function (){
    var settings = { startDelayTime: 1000, endDelayTime: 14000, itemContainer: '.registry-feature-popup', itemException: '.account-area-dropdown.registry', itemID: "RegistryNewFeature" },
    registryPrompt,
    registryPromtPopup = jQuery('.registry-feature-popup'),
    registryPromtCont = jQuery('.registry'),
    positionOfRegistry = registryPromtCont.position(),
    cookieData = function() {
        return {
            getCookieData:function(c_name){
                var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");
                for (i=0;i&lt;ARRcookies.length;i++){
                    x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
                    y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);
                    x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
                    if (x==c_name){
                        return unescape(y);
                    }
                }
            },

            setCookieData:function(c_name,value,exdays,secure){
                var exdate=new Date();
                exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
                var c_value=escape(value) + ((exdays==null) ? "" : "; expires="+exdate.toUTCString());
                var isSecure = '';
                if (secure) {
                    isSecure = '; secure;';
                } 
                document.cookie=c_name + "=" + c_value + '; path=/' + isSecure;
            },

            ifCookie:function(name){
                var cookieInfo=this.getCookieData(name);
                if (cookieInfo != null &amp;&amp; cookieInfo != "") {
                    return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        };
    },
    itemContainerPrompt = function () {

        var settings = {
            startDelayTime: 3000,
            endDelayTime: 7000,
            itemContainer: '#user-signin-prompt',
            itemClose: '.close-x',
            itemException: '#user-account',
            itemID: "UserSignIn"
        };
        var autoCloseTimer;
        var cookies = cookieData();

        return {
            init: function(set) {
                var _this = this;

                jQuery.extend(settings,set);

                settings.itemContainer = jQuery(settings.itemContainer);
                settings.itemClose = settings.itemContainer.find(settings.itemClose);
                settings.itemException = jQuery(settings.itemException);
                settings.itemID = 'sto' + settings.itemID;

                _this.checkInstance();

            },
            checkInstance: function(){
                var _this = this;

                if (!cookies.ifCookie(settings.itemID)){
                    _this.openItemPrompt();

                    settings.itemContainer.on('mouseenter',function(){
                        _this.endTimer();
                    });
                    settings.itemContainer.on('mouseleave',function(){
                        _this.startTimer();
                    });
                    settings.itemClose.on('click',function(){
                        _this.closeItemPrompt();
                    });
                    settings.itemException.on('mouseover',function(){
                        _this.closeItemPrompt();
                    }); 
                }
            },        
            openItemPrompt: function() {
                var _this = this;

                var startDelay = setTimeout(function(){
                    settings.itemContainer.fadeIn('slow');          
                    _this.startTimer();
                },settings.startDelayTime);
                cookies.setCookieData(settings.itemID, 'true', 365);
                cookies.setCookieData(settings.itemID+"secure", 'true', 365, true);

            },
            closeItemPrompt: function(action) {
                var _this = this;

                _this.endTimer();
                if (action === 'fade'){
                    settings.itemContainer.fadeOut('slow');
                }else{
                    settings.itemContainer.hide();
                }
                if (localStorage.UserSignInHidden) {
                    localStorage.removeItem('stoUserSignIn');
                    localStorage.removeItem('UserSignInHidden');
                }
                
            },
            startTimer: function(){
                var _this = this;

                autoCloseTimer = setTimeout(function(){
                    _this.closeItemPrompt('fade');
                },settings.endDelayTime);
            },
            endTimer: function() {
                clearTimeout(autoCloseTimer);
            }
        };
    },
    cookies = cookieData();
    if ($('.account-area-dropdown.registry')) {
        if(os.isLocalStorageEnabled()) {
            if ((!localStorage.stoUserSignIn &amp;&amp; !cookies.ifCookie('stoRegistryNewFeature')) || (!localStorage.stoUserSignIn &amp;&amp; !cookies.ifCookie('stoRegistryNewFeaturesecure')) ) {
                registryPromtPopup.css('left', positionOfRegistry.left-45);
                localStorage.setItem('stoUserSignIn', 'true');
                localStorage.setItem('UserSignInHidden', 'true');
                registryPrompt = itemContainerPrompt();
                registryPrompt.init(settings);
            }
        }
        if ((!cookies.ifCookie('stoRegistryNewFeature') &amp;&amp; localStorage.stoUserSignIn) || (!cookies.ifCookie('stoRegistryNewFeaturesecure') &amp;&amp; localStorage.stoUserSignIn) &amp;&amp; registryPromtPopup &amp;&amp; registryPromtPopup.length&gt;0 ) {
            registryPromtPopup.css('left', positionOfRegistry.left-45);
            registryPrompt = itemContainerPrompt();
            registryPrompt.init(settings);
        }    
    }
});
   </script>

   <script>
    if(jQuery('#home-page').length &gt; 0){

    // Google Analytics on Add To Cart Button, move to external js asap

    $('#addCartMain_addCartButton').on('click', function(e) {
        var $this = $(this);
        var gaSession = ga.trackingManager.getTrackingSessions();
        var $selectQty = $('input[name*="addqty"]').val();
        var getOptionId = function(){
            var product = os.productpage;
            var $dropdownVal = $('.options-dropdown').val();

            if(product.hasMultipleOptions &amp;&amp; $dropdownVal) {
                return $('.options-dropdown').val();
            }
            else if (product.hasMultipleOptions &amp;&amp; !$dropdownVal) {
                return '';
            }
            else {
                return product.defaultOption.id;
            }
        };
        var obj = {};
        obj.sessions = [];
        obj.products = [];

        //build data object by looping through gaSession
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; gaSession.length; i++) {
            obj.sessions.push(gaSession[i]);
        }
        var tempObj = {
            optionId: parseInt(getOptionId()),
            quantity: parseInt($selectQty)
        }
        obj.products.push(tempObj);
        if(getOptionId() &amp;&amp; gaSession) {
            $.ajax({
                url: 'http://www.overstock.com/api2/tracking/events/carts/products',
                data: JSON.stringify(obj),
                type: 'POST',
                contentType: 'application/json'
            }).done(function(data) {
                //
            }).error(function(data) {
                //
            });
        }

    });

    
    


function getGoogleAdSense() {
//console.log('google adsense function');
  if(!os.productpage.isAdult &amp;&amp; typeof _googCsa != 'undefined'){
  	displayGoogleAdSense();
  }else{
    jQuery('#GOOGLE_ADS_PP_CONTAINER').hide();
    //console.log('ads hidden');
  }

}

function displayGoogleAdSense(){
    var srchKeyword = _.unescape(os.productpage.productName);
    //console.log('google run', srchKeyword);

    os.googleAdSense = {};

    os.googleAdSense.pageOptions = {
      'pubId'        : 'partner-vert-pla-overstock-pdp',
      'query'        : String(srchKeyword),
      'adsafe'       : 'high',
      'channel'      : 'untracked',
      'hl'           : 'en',
      'adtest'       : 'off',
      'linkTarget'   : '_blank'
    };

    os.googleAdSense.block = {
      'container' : 'afshcontainer',
      'width'     : 960,
      'height'    : 300,
      'promoted'  : false
    };

    _googCsa('plas', os.googleAdSense.pageOptions, os.googleAdSense.block);
}

    //DEV_API_SET_COOKIE

(function(){
    var url = window.location.href;
    if(url.match(/\?./)){
	//Check parameter on product pages to see if user has siteID in url
	var urlParam = JSON.parse('{"' + decodeURIComponent(location.search.substring(1).replace(/%20&amp;%20/g,'%20%26%20').replace(/&amp;/g, "\",\"").replace(/=/g, "\":\"")) + '"}');
	if(urlParam.siteID){
		Object.defineProperty(Date.prototype, 'YYYYMMDDHHMM', {
    		value: function() {
        		function pad2(n) {  // always returns a string
            		return (n &lt; 10 ? '0' : '') + n;
        		}
        		//console.log(this);
        		return this.getFullYear() +
            		pad2(this.getMonth() + 1) + 
            		pad2(this.getDate()) +
            		pad2(this.getHours()) +
            		pad2(this.getMinutes());
    		}
		});

		var getEnsiDate = new Date().YYYYMMDDHHMM();
		function splitValue(value, index) {
    		return value.substring(0, index) + "_" + value.substring(index);
		}
		var ensiDate = splitValue(getEnsiDate, 8);
		//console.log(ensiDate);
		//Set or reset cookie data
	        os.standardCookieData().setCookieData('devAPI','{"storeTime":"'+ensiDate+'","siteID":"'+urlParam.siteID+'"}',90);

	}
    }
}());

function addSegmentEvent() {
	var segmentNum = os.Otags.segment;

	if(segmentNum &gt;= 62 &amp;&amp; segmentNum &lt;= 65) {
		if(!s.events) {
			s.events = 'event62';
		} else {
			s.events = s.events + ',event62';
		}
	}
}

	addSegmentEvent();
}
